CMS Research Data and Assistance Center (ResDAC)

Interface Overview

The University of Hawaii (UH) will act as the requesting agency and submit annual (and as needed) requests for refreshes/updates of Medicare Enrollment, Fee-for-Service Claims, and Encounters data, as well as Medicaid Enrollment, Claims, and Encounters data, to the CMS Research Data and Assistance Center (ResDAC) at the University of Minnesota through the State Agency Request Program.

File Details

This interface covers multiple CMS claim-level and beneficiary-level datasets provided via ResDAC. Each table below lists the column name, a short description, and the source data type/length as received. Field names are preserved from source and may contain underscores or CMS abbreviations. All personally identifiable information (PII) or protected health information (PHI) must be handled according to State and Federal policy.

Consists of Medicare Fee-for-Service Research Identifiable Files (RIFs) obtained through CMS State Agency Request authority. These files contain detailed Medicare claims and enrollment information for beneficiaries in HawaiК»i and support longitudinal analyses of healthcare access, quality, utilization, and outcomes among older adults and individuals with disabilities.

Data Transfer Overview

Security and Privacy Constraints

ConstraintRequirement
Highest HAP PHI Classification LevelLevel 3 - Confidential
Retention Requirements7 years

File Layout

All data files submitted via the CMS ResDAC interface will follow the specifications below.

File Naming Conventions:

  • Control File: resdac_control_pulldate(CCYYMMDD).cnt

    • Example: resdac_control_20230831.cnt

  • Data Files: tabletype_tablename_year(YYYY)_timestamp(CCYYMMDDhhmmss).txt

    • Example: df_bcarrier_claims_2010_20230831.txt

  • Characteristics Files: tabletype_tablename_year(YYYY)_timestamp(CCYYMMDDhhmmss).txt

    • Example: cf_excl_drugs_2010_20230831.txt

  • Reference Files: tabletype_tablename_timestamp(CCYYMMDDhhmmss).txt

    • Example: rf_betos_codes_20230831.txt
